***купить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́ть</a> (576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kupiti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kupítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покупать.html>покупа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to buy, to purchase
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a> кое-что́ <b><a href = vnd.unilang:купить.html>купи́ть</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja xočú koje-štó <b>kupítʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I want <b>to buy</b> something.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="геометрическое">геометр.</span> подкласс призматоидов, <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соединённый.html>соединённых</a> многоугольника, <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́ром</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:основание.html>основа́ние</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдвое.html>вдво́е</a> больше <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сторо́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнение.html>сравне́нию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́м</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:верхний.html>ве́рхняя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грань.html>грань</a>); <a href = vnd.unilang:призма.html>при́зму</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> многоугольников <a href = vnd.unilang:наполовину.html>наполови́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стянуть.html>стя́нут</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объединение.html>объедине́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вершина.html>верши́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:попарно.html>попа́рно</a></ol>

***кур.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>кур</a> (24374)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">куръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kurъ</i>. The normal word for the rooster in Old Russian, displaced from the 17<sup>th</sup> century by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пѣту́хъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pětúx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>кур</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kur</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кура.html>ку́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кур.html>ку́ров</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куриный.html>кури́ный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now  rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rooster, cock</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cour</i>, and constructions with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">délatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and the like from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">faire la cour</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>кур</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kur</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кура.html>ку́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кур.html>ку́ров</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mostly with verbs <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a></i> and less often <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></i>, and both in the singular and as a  pluraletantum</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[18<sup>th</sup> c. to mid 19<sup>th</sup> c.]</span>
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Russian-faire_la_cour"> attention which one pays to someone, gloze
<ol><li>in diplomatic affairs, accolading, formal address</li>
<li>to a woman, wooing, cajoling
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1769</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Denis_Fonvizin" class="extiw" title="w:Denis Fonvizin">Dennis <a href = vnd.unilang:вон.html>von</a> Wiesen</a>,  <cite>Бригадиръ</cite>, 2, 6:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> увѣрена, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> онъ <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́шу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деревня.html>дере́вню</a> предпочтетъ <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рай.html>раю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> Парижу; <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́вом</a>, <b>онъ мнѣ дѣлаетъ <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a> куръ</b>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja óčenʹ uvěrena, što on nášu derévnju predpočtet i raju, i Parižu; slóvom, <b>on mně dělajet svoj kur</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I am very confident that he will prefer our village over both paradise and Paris; in a word, <b>he is wooing me</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1790</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yakov_Knyazhnin" class="extiw" title="w:Yakov Knyazhnin"><a href = vnd.unilang:як.html>я́ков</a> бори́сович княжни́н</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:чудак.html>Чудаки́</a></cite>, 2, 3:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>Хочу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a>, ciel!<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> томъ <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> tous mes voeux! … <a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>Сама́</a> Agnes Sorel<br />Французскимъ королемъ такъ <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любимый.html>люби́ма</a>,<br />Какъ <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мно́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́ша</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дочь.html>дочь</a>. — Je jurerai toujours,<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> дѣлая <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ей</a> куръ</b>,<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> тѣмъ <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> сдѣлаю нималаго <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <span class="None" lang="fr">крима</span>:<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>Она</a> divinité!</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Xoču li ja? o, ciel!<br />V tom tolʹko tous mes voeux! … Sama Agnes Sorel<br />Francuzskim korolem tak ta byla ljubima,<br />Kak mnoju vaša dočʹ. — Je jurerai toujours,<br />Što ja mogu skazatʹ, <b>ne dělaja jej kur</b>,<br />I těm ne sdělaju nimalago ja <span class="None" lang="fr">krima</span>:<br />Ona divinité!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Do I want to? oh, heavens!<br />That's just all I wish! … Agnes Sorel herself<br />Was so beloved of the French king,<br />As your daughter is by me. “I will always swear<br />That I can say <b>without wooing her</b>,<br />And so I will not commit a trivial crime:<br />She is divinity!”</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1815</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mikhail_Zagoskin" class="extiw" title="w:Mikhail Zagoskin">михаи́л никола́евич заго́скин</a>,  <cite>Комедія противъ комедіи, <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> урокъ волокитамъ</cite>, 1, 1:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Софья</span>. Онъ <a href = vnd.unilang:искренний.html>и́скренно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> любитъ.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em"><a href = vnd.unilang:княгиня.html>Княги́ня</a></span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:искренний.html>И́скренно</a> любитъ–графъ Фольгинъ! <a href = vnd.unilang:ха.html>ха</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ха.html>ха</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ха.html>ха</a>!  Ахъ! ma chère, <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видно.html>видно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жила</a> въ свѣтѣ.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Софья.</span> Почему-жъ <a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>ка́жется</a> вамъ <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> невѣроятнымъ? <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> имѣю <a href = vnd.unilang:никакой.html>никако́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причина.html>причи́ны</a> сомнѣваться въ <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:искренность.html>и́скренности</a>.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em"><a href = vnd.unilang:княгиня.html>Княги́ня</a></span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>О</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конечно.html>коне́чно</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:странный.html>Стра́нно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> графъ, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотря́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:искренний.html>и́скреннюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вь</a> къ тебѣ, <a href = vnd.unilang:стараться.html>стара́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> увѣрять въ томъ-же; <b>дѣлаетъ <a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>куры</a> тетушкѣ</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волочиться.html>волочится</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a>…<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Даша</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мно́ю</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> почему-жъ <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> такъ, <a href = vnd.unilang:сударыня.html>суда́рыня</a>, вѣдь <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщина</a>.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Софья</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>Э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a> вѣтренность. <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> увѣрена, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> графъ любитъ <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одну́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em"><a href = vnd.unilang:княгиня.html>Княги́ня</a></span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>Или</a> можетъ <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:богатый.html>бога́тое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приданое.html>прида́ное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тетушка.html>тётушка</a> даетъ <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тобо́ю</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Sofʹja</span>. On iskrenno menja ljubit.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Knjaginja</span>. Iskrenno ljubit–graf Folʹgin! xa, xa, xa!  Ax! ma chère, očenʹ vidno, što ty ješče ne žila v světě.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Sofʹja.</span> Počemu-ž kažetsja vam eto nevěrojatnym? Ja ne iměju nikakoj pričiny somněvatʹsja v jevo iskrennosti.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Knjaginja</span>. O konečno! Stranno tolʹko, što graf, ne smotrja na svoju iskrennjuju ljubovʹ k tebě, starajetsja menja uvěrjatʹ v tom-že; <b>dělajet kury tetuškě</b>, i voločitsja daže…<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Daša</span>. Za mnoju. Da počemu-ž i ne tak, sudarynja, vědʹ i ja takže ženščina.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Sofʹja</span>. Eto lišʹ větrennostʹ. Ja uvěrena, što graf ljubit odnu menja.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Knjaginja</span>. Ili možet bytʹ bogatoje pridanoje, kotoroje tetuška dajet za toboju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Sophie</span>. He genuinely loves me.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Duchess</span>. Count Folgin loves genuinely?! Ha, ha, ha!  Ah! My dear, it is really transparent that you haven’t lived in the world.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Sophie.</span> Why do you deem it improbable? I have no reason to doubt his sincerity.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Duchess</span>. Sure! Curious though that the count, not regarding his genuine love for you, strives to persuade me of the same; <b>he woos auntie</b>, and even chases after her…<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Dora</span>. After me? And why not, madam, since I am likewise a woman?<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Sophie</span>. This is merely flightiness. I am certain that the count loves me alone.<br /><span style="letter-spacing:0.2em">Duchess</span>. Or it might be the rich dowry that auntie gives with you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волочиться.html>волочи́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">voločítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***курва.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:курва.html>ку́рва</a> (16283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:курва.html>ку́рва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prostitute, whore</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kury</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whore</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kurъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bird, hen; cock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курва.html>ку́рва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kúrva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курва.html>ку́рвы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курва.html>ку́рвы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курва.html>ку́рв</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>whore, prostitute</li>
<li>bitch, slut</li>
<li>bastard</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кургузый.html>кургу́зый</a> (20869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">*кърногузъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*kŭrnoguzŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">*кърнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*kŭrnŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cut, chopped</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">гуз</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">guz</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">buttocks, rump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кургузый.html>кургу́зый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kurgúzyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dock-tailed, bobtail, shorthaired <i>(of an animal)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> too tight, too short <i>(of clothing)</i>

Latn">Na malenʹkoj golovke žokejskij kartuzik, kletčatyj kurguzyj vozdušnyj že pidžačok… Graždanin rostom v saženʹ, no v plečax uzok, xud neimoverno, i fizionomija, prošu zametitʹ, glumlivaja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">On his small head was a jockey-cap and he wore a short check bum-freezer made of air. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курение.html>куре́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kurénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курение.html>куре́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курение.html>куре́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курение.html>куре́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>smoking (verbal noun, the smoking of tobacco)</li>
<li>incense</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:курилка.html>кури́лка</a> (17414)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to smoke</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***куриный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:куриный.html>кури́ный</a> (7727)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>кур</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kur</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ínyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куриный.html>кури́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kurínyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chicken
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:куриный.html>кури́ный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бульон.html>бульо́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kurínyj</b> bulʹón</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>chicken</b> broth</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:куриный.html>кури́ные</a></b> бёдрышки</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kurínyje</b> bjódryški</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>chicken</b> thighs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>limited, narrow-minded
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:куриный.html>кури́ный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ум.html>ум</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kurínyj</b> um</i> ― <span class="e-translation">closed mind</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">chicken mind</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:куриный.html>кури́ная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:логика.html>ло́гика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kurínaja</b> lógika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">narrow-minded logic</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">chicken logic</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***курительный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:курительный.html>кури́тельный</a> (25612)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курительный.html>кури́тельный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kurítelʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> smoking
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:курительный.html>кури́тельная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мната</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kurítelʹnaja</b> kómnata</i> ― <span class="e-translation">smoking room</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:курительный.html>кури́тельный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:табак.html>таба́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kurítelʹnyj</b> tabák</i> ― <span class="e-translation">smoking tobacco</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***курить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a> (1210)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кꙋрити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kuriti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">smoke, emit smoke</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kuriti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kurítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покурить.html>покури́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smoke (tobacco etc.)</li>
<li>to burn, to fumigate</li>
<li>to distil</li></ol>

***куриться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:куриться.html>кури́ться</a> (17399)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куриться.html>кури́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kurítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to smoke, to emit smoke, to fume</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:куриться.html>ку́рится</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú ne <b>kúritsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is not in the smoking mood</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***курица.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рица</a> (4667)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kurica</i>, equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кура.html>ку́ра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ица</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рица</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kúrica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рицы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́ры</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рицы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>кур</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́риц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>chicken (a bird of species <i>Gallus gallus</i>).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рица</a></b> — <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:птица.html>пти́ца</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:баба.html>ба́ба</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">derisive proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kúrica</b> — ne ptíca, bába — ne čelovék.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A chicken is not a bird and a woman is not a human.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рица</a></b> — <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:птица.html>пти́ца</a>, по́льша — <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заграница.html>заграни́ца</a>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">derisive proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kúrica</b> — ne ptíca, Pólʹša — ne zagraníca.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A chicken is not a bird and Poland is not a foreign country.<br /><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Poland here may be replaced by any other formerly socialist country or former Soviet republic.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>hen <i>(female chicken)</i>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рица</a></b> кло́хчет (<a href = vnd.unilang:кудахтать.html>куда́хчет</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kúrica</b> klóxčet (kudáxčet)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a hen cackles (clucks)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́ры</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нестись.html>несу́тся</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kúry nesútsja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hens lay eggs</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рица</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:снести.html>снесла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>яйцо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kúrica</b> sneslá jajcó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a hen has laid an egg</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рица</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:высиживать.html>выси́живает</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>я́йца</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kúrica</b> vysíživajet jájca</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> hen is brooding</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>chicken <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">flesh of a chicken used as food</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:курносый.html>курно́сый</a> (9912)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кърноносый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kŭrnonosyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with a cut nose</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">корнать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kornatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">корноухий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kornouxij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курносый.html>курно́сый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kurnósyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pug-nosed, snub-nosed</li>
<li><i>(nose)</i> turned-up</li></ol>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="выступает в роли существительного">субстантивир.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:короткий.html>коро́ткий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вздернутый.html>вздёрнутый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>нос</a> <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>кур</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kur</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>куро́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kurók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курок.html>курка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курок.html>курки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курок.html>курко́в</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:куропатка.html>куропа́тка</a> (18980)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кура.html>кура</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kura</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (a shortened form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рица</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúrica</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + Old East Slavic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пъта</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pŭta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the current form of which is <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:птица.html>пти́ца</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ptíca</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bird</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куропатка.html>куропа́тка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kuropátka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куропатка.html>куропа́тки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куропатка.html>куропа́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куропатка.html>куропа́ток</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:курорт.html>куро́рт</a> (6308)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kurort</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курорт.html>куро́рт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kurórt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курорт.html>куро́рта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курорт.html>куро́рты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курорт.html>куро́ртов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курортный.html>куро́ртный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>resort, holiday resort, health resort</li></ol>
